echo "Filter Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    filter 
        ip-filter 1001 create
            description "pre-vod-ingress" 
            entry 10 create
                match 
                    dst-ip ip-prefix-list "pre-vod"
                exit 
                action
                    forward
                exit
            exit 
        exit 
        ip-filter 1002 create
            description "pre-vod-egress" 
            entry 10 create
                match 
                    src-ip ip-prefix-list "pre-vod"
                exit 
                action
                    forward
                exit
            exit 
        exit 
        mac-filter 10 create
            description "pre-vod-ingress" 
            type vid
            entry 10 create
                match frame-type ethernet_II
                    inner-tag 43 4095
                exit 
                action
                    forward
                exit
            exit 
        exit 
    exit
